- "Heavy movement" - Distracting from product

ğŸ—ºï¸ REAL LOCATIONS (TIKTOK SHOP ADAPTATION)
================================================

**RULE:** Use REAL verifiable locations when possible, generic HOME descriptions allowed for privacy.

**TIKTOK SHOP SPECIFICITY:**
- **Public venues** (cafes, studios, beaches): Must be REAL with names
- **Private spaces** (home, bedroom, fitting room): Can use generic descriptions for privacy
- **Reason:** Sellers often film at home (can't publicize address), but public spaces should be real

**âœ… CORRECT FOR TIKTOK SHOP:**

**Public Venues (Real names required):**
- "The Coffee House - Bright corner, Nguyen Hue, District 1" (real cafe)
- "Tiá»‡m CÃ  PhÃª Apartment - Minimalist room, Nguyen Hue, District 1"

- "Clean home living room - Bright neutral decor"
- "Private fitting room - Full-length mirror, white walls"
- "Home studio - White backdrop, ring light setup"

**Format for Public:**
```
"[Venue Name] - [Area], [Address/District]"
```

**Format for Private:**
```
"[Generic Space Type] - [Key Features]"
```

**EXAMPLES BY TIER:**

**Tier A (Studio/Fitting Room) - Mostly private:**
- "Private home studio - White backdrop, professional lighting"

**Tier C (Lifestyle) - Mostly public:**

**AVOID:**
- Publishing exact home addresses (privacy)

- Overly specific private details

================================================
ğŸ’¡ TIKTOK SHOP LIGHTING PRIORITIES
================================================

**TOP 3 LIGHTING SETUPS:**

**1. Natural Window Light (â­â­â­â­â­ Best):**
- **Setup:** Model facing large window, soft diffused daylight
- **Why:** Free, flattering, feels authentic
- **Best time:** 9AM-11AM or 2PM-4PM (avoid harsh noon)
- **Add:** White reflector opposite window for fill
- **Result:** Soft, natural, trustworthy vibe

**2. Ring Light + Natural (â­â­â­â­ Professional):**
- **Setup:** Ring light front, window light side/back
- **Why:** Even lighting, good for close-ups, seller standard
- **Settings:** 50-70% brightness, warm 3200K-4000K
- **Result:** Professional seller look, beauty lighting

**3. Softbox 2-Point (â­â­â­ Studio):**
- **Setup:** Key light 45Â° front-left, fill light 45Â° front-right
- **Why:** Full control, consistent across videos
- **Settings:** Key 100%, Fill 50-60%
- **Result:** Studio professional, E-commerce standard

**AVOID:**
- âŒ Harsh overhead ceiling light â†’ unflattering shadows
- âŒ Yellow tungsten bulbs â†’ bad color, looks cheap
- âŒ Too dark moody lighting â†’ TikTok penalty
- âŒ Backlit silhouette â†’ can't see product

**BRIGHTNESS CHECK:**
â†’ Video should look sli slightly brighter than real life
â†’ All product details clearly visible
â†’ No harsh shadows on face

================================================
ğŸ“¸ TIKTOK SHOP CAMERA SETUP
================================================

**CAMERA DISTANCE & FRAMING:**
- **Full body shots:** Camera 2-3 meters away
- **3/4 body:** Camera 1.5-2 meters
- **Upper body:** Camera 1-1.5 meters
- **Close-up details:** Camera 0.5-1 meter

**CRITICAL:** Always show ENOUGH of product
â†’ If selling dress, must see from shoulder to hem
â†’ Don't crop too tight cutting off product

**ANGLE PRIORITY:**
1. **Eye level** (â­â­â­â­â­) - Most flattering, natural
2. **Slight low angle** (â­â­â­â­) - TÃ´n dÃ¡ng, legs look longer
3. **High angle** (â­â­) - Only for specific products

**FRAMING RULE:**
- 70% Model + Product
- 30% Background (clean, supporting)
- Leave breathing room top and bottom
- For TikTok 9:16: Vertical optimization

**STABILITY:**
- âœ… Tripod or stable surface
- âŒ Handheld shaky (unless intentional POV)
- Smooth camera if moving

ğŸ“‹ TIKTOK SHOP SCENE STRUCTURE OPTIMIZATION
================================================

**4 SCENES CHO TIKTOK SHOP (32s):**

**SCENE 1 (0-8s): HOOK + PRODUCT REVEAL**

**SCENE 2 (8-16s): SIZE + QUALITY PROOF**

**SCENE 3 (16-24s): FIT + BENEFIT**

- **Motion:** Hand on waist OR pose showing fit
- **Script:** "Máº·c vÃ o Ã´m dÃ¡ng/thoáº£i mÃ¡i, tÃ´n lÃªn [benefit]!"
- **Goal:** Show how it looks on body, benefits

**SCENE 4 (24-32s): URGENCY + CTA**
- **Environment:** Same
- **Camera:** Static or slight zoom out

- **Script:** "Chá»‰ cÃ²n X sáº£n pháº©m! Link bÃªn dÆ°á»›i, chá»‘t ngay!"
- **Goal:** Create urgency, drive to cart

**ENVIRONMENT CONSISTENCY:**
â†’ Keep same location all 4 scenes
â†’ Change only camera angle/distance
â†’ Maintains focus, looks professional

ğŸ“Š CVR OPTIMIZATION CHECKLIST
================================================

âš ï¸ VEO 3.1 FALLBACK OPTIONS (Káº¾ HOáº CH Dá»° PHÃ’NG)
================================================
**Má»¤C ÄÃCH:** Khi Veo 3.1 fail motion phá»©c táº¡p, cÃ³ backup plan.

**ğŸ”„ MOTION FALLBACK HIERARCHY:**

**360Â° SPIN FAIL:**
1. Thá»­ láº¡i vá»›i "slower rotation, 6 seconds for full spin"
2. Fallback to 180Â° spin: "Half rotation showing front and back"
3. Fallback to pivot: "Standing pivot turn 90Â° left then right"
4. Ultimate fallback: Static pose + camera orbit

**WALKING FAIL:**
1. Thá»­ láº¡i vá»›i "2-3 short steps forward only"
2. Fallback to pivot walk: "Weight shift left-right in place"

**SIT-STAND FAIL:**
1. Thá»­ láº¡i vá»›i "slow controlled sitting motion over 4 seconds"
2. Fallback to half motion: "Beginning to sit, stopping at knee bend"
3. Fallback to lean: "Leaning on chair arm instead of sitting"

**FABRIC TOUCH FAIL:**
1. Thá»­ láº¡i vá»›i "static hand position on fabric"
2. Fallback: "One hand resting on hip"
3. Ultimate fallback: "Arms naturally at sides"

**COMPLEX COMBO FAIL:**
1. Break into single actions: "First spin, then touch fabric"
2. Fallback: Remove one action, keep simpler one
3. Ultimate fallback: Static pose with camera movement

**ğŸ“‹ FALLBACK REPLACEMENT TABLE:**
| Original Motion | Fallback Level 1 | Fallback Level 2 | Fallback Level 3 |
|----------------|------------------|------------------|------------------|
| 360Â° spin | 180Â° slow turn | Pivot 90Â° | Static + camera orbit |
| 4+ step walk | 2 step walk | Weight shift | Static + push in |
| Sit â†’ Stand | Lean â†’ Straighten | Half squat | Static seated |
| Squat | Knee bend | Hip shift | Standing |
| Jump | Bounce on toes | Weight shift | Static energetic pose |
| Hair flip | Hand near hair | Touch shoulder | Arms relaxed |
| Wave | Subtle hand raise | Fingers wiggle | Static friendly pose |

**ğŸ¬ REGENERATION PROMPT ADJUSTMENTS:**
